   pramāṇāntaram eveti bhāvaḥ / kathaṃ vā na syād ity ācāryaḥ /	pramANa-antaram eva-iti BAvaH / kaTam vA na syAt iti AcAryaH /
   dṛṣṭāntānapekṣaṇād iti paraḥ / dṛṣṭāntāpekṣaṃ hy anumānam	dRzwAnta-anapekzaNAt iti paraH / dRzwAnta-apekzam hi anumAnam
   anvayavyatirekava .. ///	anvaya-vyatirekavaH .. ///
   3 /// .. .. .. .. mānaṃ dṛṣṭāntānapekṣatām edva na hītyādinā prāha / asyām	3 /// .. .. .. .. mAnam dRzwAnta-anapekza-tAm edva na hi-ityAdinA prAha / asyAm
   ity anupalabdhau kiṃ na nirupākhyam ityādi ācāryaḥ dṛṣṭānta evety arthaḥ /	iti anupalabDO kim na nirupAKyam ityAdi AcAryaH dRzwAntaH eva-iti arTaH /
   tad asad ityādi paraḥ / tad vyomakusumādi asad iti kathaṃ kena	tat asat ityAdi paraH / tat vyoma-kusuma-Adi asat iti kaTam kena
   pramāṇenāvagantavyaṃ yenaivaṃ syāt* / anupalaabdher liṅgād abhāve sādhye	pramANena-avagantavyam yena-evam syAt* / anupalaabDeH liFgAt aBAve sADye
   dṛṣṭāntaḥ syād ity arthaḥ / anupalabdher eva liṅgād vyomakusumā ///	dRzwAntaH syAt iti arTaH / anupalabDeH eva liFgAt vyomakusumAH ///
   4 /// .idyate dṛṣṭānto yasyā asattāsiddher iti vigrahaḥ / athātrāpy aparo	4 /// .idyate dRzwAntaH yasyAH asattA-sidDeH iti vigrahaH / aTa-atra-api aparaH-
   dṛṣṭāntas tasyā vyomakusumādyasattāsiddheḥ sadṛṣṭāntatve	dRzwAntaH tasyAH vyoma-kusuma-Adi-asattA-sidDeH sa-dRzwAnta-tve
   vānavasthāprasaṃgaḥ / tatrāpy aparo dṛṣṭāntas tatrāpy aparo 'pīti kṛtvā /	vAnavasTA-prasaMgaH / tatra-api aparaH dRzwAntaH tatra-api aparaH api-iti kRtvA /
   tathā cānavasthāyāṃ satyāṃ ekasyāpi siddhāv apratipattiḥ / sarvatra tasmād	taTA ca-anavasTAyAm satyAm ekasya-api sidDO apratipattiH / sarvatra tasmAt-
   anavasthādoṣaparihārārthaṃ nirupākhya ///	anavasTA-doza-parihAra-arTam nirupAKya ///
   5 /// .. labdhilakṣaṇaprāptasya anupalabdher ityādāv api prayoge	5 /// .. labDi-lakzaNa-prAptasya anupalabDeH iti-AdO api prayoge
   dṛṣṭāntānapekṣaṇād ananumānam anupalabdhiḥ / śṛṇvann apīty ācāryaḥ / sakṛd	dRzwAnta-anapekzaNAt ananumAnam anupalabDiH / SRNvan api-iti AcAryaH / sakRt-
   uktaṃ yathā svabhāvānupalabdhau nābhāvaḥ sādhyate kiṃtu abhāvavyavahāra	uktam yaTA svaBAva-anupalabDO na-aBAvaH sADyate kiMtu aBAva-vyavahAra
   iti tacchṛṇvann api / mūrkhasya trīṇi nāmāni devo divyaḥ prajayatir ity	iti tat-SRNvan api / mUrKasya trINi nAmAni devaH divyaH prajayatiH iti-
   ato devānāṃ mūrkhāṇāṃ pri .. ///	atas devAnAm mUrKANAm pri .. ///
   6 /// ..m evāsadvyavahāraṃ sādhyaṃ darśayann āha / nimittaṃ hītyādi /	6 /// ..m eva-asat-vyavahAram sADyam darSayan Aha / nimittam hi-ityAdi /
   dṛśyasyānupalabdhir upalabhyānupalabdhiḥ / sā nimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ	dRSyasya-anupalabDiH upalaBya-anupalabDiH / sA nimittam kAraNam
   sadvyavahārāṇāṃ sānupalabdhiḥ svasannidhānād ātmanā sannidhānāt* /	sat-vyavahArANAm sa-anupalabDiH sva-sanniDAnAt AtmanA sanniDAnAt* /
   svanimittān* svam anupalabdhirūpa .. ///	sva-nimittAn* svam anupalabDi-rUpaH .. ///
